--- Commit Message ---
LU-17327 tests: conf-sanity/46b to avoid MDT balance

Check if disabling LMV QOS avoids newly-added MDTs
from being allocated to new files/dirs while being
added to the filesystem.

Test-Parameters: fortestonly
Test-Parameters: testlist=conf-sanity env=ONLY=46b,ONLY_REPEAT=5,SLOW=yes mdtcount=8 mdscount=2
